build-not-bin-vergil:
     [echo] 
     [echo] 	$PTII/bin/vergil does not exist, perhaps (cd $PTII/bin; make) has not been run?
     [echo] 	This can happen if the make binary cannot be found in the path or if $PTII/mk/ptII.mk
     [echo] 	is not present.
     [echo] 	Skipping running make in $PTII/bin, which creates scripts like $PTII/bin/vergil.
     [echo] 	This is only an issue if you want to invoke "$PTII/bin/vergil" instead of "ant vergil".
     [echo] 	However, $PTII/bin does include other scripts that may be of use.
     [echo]

    [junit] 	# In general, if we call getName on a public field in an actor,
    [junit] 	# then the name that is returned should be the same as the name
    [junit] 	# of the field.
    [junit] 	set entityList [$configuration allAtomicEntityList]
    [junit] 	set results {}
    [junit] 	for {set iterator [$entityList iterator]}  {[$iterator hasNext] == 1} {} {
    [junit] 		set entity [$iterator next]
    [junit] 		if [java::instanceof $entity ptolemy.actor.TypedAtomicActor] {
    [junit] 		    set actor [java::cast ptolemy.actor.TypedAtomicActor $entity]
    [junit] 		    set className [$actor getClassName]
    [junit] 		    set url [java::call ptolemy.vergil.actor.DocManager  docClassNameToURL  $configuration $className  true false false false]
    [junit] 		    if [java::isnull $url] {
    [junit] 			lappend results "\nFailed to find ptdoc for $className.  Try doing (cd $PTII/doc; rm codeDoc/ptolemy/actor/lib/Ramp.xml codeDoc/ptolemy/actor/lib/RampIdx.xml; make docs)"
    [junit] 		    }
    [junit] 
    [junit] 
    [junit] 		    set url [java::call ptolemy.vergil.actor.DocManager  docClassNameToURL  $configuration $className  false true false false]
    [junit] 		    if [java::isnull $url] {
    [junit] 			lappend results "\nFailed to find javadoc for $className"
    [junit] 		    }
    [junit] 
    [junit] 		    set url [java::call ptolemy.vergil.actor.DocManager  docClassNameToURL  $configuration $className  false true false false]
    [junit] 		    if [java::isnull $url] {
    [junit] 			lappend results "\nFailed to find source for $className"
    [junit] 		    }
    [junit] 
    [junit] 
    [junit] 		    # For actor index, it is ok to return null
    [junit] 		    set url [java::call ptolemy.vergil.actor.DocManager  docClassNameToURL  $configuration $className  false false false true]
